<script>

    function saveSession(sport) 
    {
        $.ajax({
			url: 'sess.php',
			type: "POST",
			data: {sport_s: sport},
			success: function() {
				window.location.reload(true);
			}
		});
		
    }

</script>

<script>
$(function() {
	$('body').addClass('collapsed');
	$('.nav-toggle').on('click', function() {
		if ($('#main-navigation').hasClass('expanded')) {
			$('#main-navigation').toggleClass('expanded');
			$('body').toggleClass('expanded');
			document.cookie = "leftBar=collapsed; path=/; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT";
		} else {
			$('#main-navigation').toggleClass('expanded');
			$('body').toggleClass('expanded');
			document.cookie = "leftBar=expanded; path=/; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT";
		}
	});
	$('.nav-comp-toggle').on('click', function() {
		$('.nav-sports').hide();
		$('.nav-comps').animate({width: 'toggle'});
	});
	$('.nav-sport-toggle').on('click', function() {
		$('.nav-comps').hide();
		$('.nav-sports').animate({width: 'toggle'});
	});
	$('.nav-sport').on('click', function() {
		var sport = $(this).data('id');
		$.ajax({
			url: 'sess.php',
			type: "POST",
			data: {sport_s: sport},
			success: function() {
				window.location.reload(true);
			}
		});
	});
	
	$('.nav-search input').on('input', function() {
		var val = $(this).val().toLowerCase();
		var items = $(this).parent().parent().find('.nav-item-wrapper > *');
		
		if (val != '') {
			items.hide();
			
			items.each(function(el) {
				if ($(this).text().toLowerCase().indexOf(val) >= 0) {
					$(this).show();
				}
			});
		} else {
			items.show();
		}
	});
});

</script>

				<input class="start_date_year" type="text" name="start_date_year[29]" maxlength="4" style="width:50px;background-color:#F0F0FF;" value=""></input></span></div></div><div class='wrap-box'><input type="hidden" name="abgeschickt" value="1"></input><input type="Submit" value="Send Data"></input></div></div></form><script type="text/javascript" src="https://code.jquery.com/jquery-1.9.1.min.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript" src="https://code.jquery.com/ui/1.10.1/jquery-ui.min.js"></script>	
<script type="text/javascript">
$(function() {
	$(".auto").autocomplete({
		source: "./internal/autosearch_city.php",
		minLength: 2
	});	
	
	function processDate() {
		var day = $('#fill_day').val();
		var month = $('#fill_month').val() - 1;
		var year = $('#fill_year').val();	
		var date  = new Date();
		date.setFullYear(year, month, day);
		var _day = date.getDate();
		var _month = date.getMonth();
		var _year = date.getFullYear();
		
		if (parseInt(day) == _day && parseInt(month) == _month && parseInt(year) == _year) {
			console.log('valid');
			$('.start_date_day').val($('#fill_day').val());
			$('.start_date_month').val($('#fill_month').val());
			$('.start_date_year').val($('#fill_year').val());
		}
	}
		
	$("#fill_nat").on('click', function() {
		$('.nationality').val($('#fill_nat_value').val());
		processDate();
	});
		
	$(".change-unit").on('click', function() {
		$('.weight').toggle();
		$('.weight_lbs').toggle();
		$('.height').toggle();
		$('.height_ft').toggle();
		$('.height_in').toggle();
	});
	
	$('.weight_lbs').on('input', function() {
		if ($(this).val() > 0) {
			$(this).parent().find('.weight').val(Math.round($(this).val() / 2.2046));
		} else {
			$(this).parent().find('.weight').val('');
		}	
	});
	$('.weight').on('input', function() {
		if ($(this).val() > 0) {
			$(this).parent().find('.weight_lbs').val(Math.round($(this).val() * 2.2046));
		} else {
			$(this).parent().find('.weight_lbs').val('');
		}	
	});
	
	
	$('.height_ft,.height_in').on('input', function() {	
		var ft = $(this).parent().find('.height_ft').val() > 0 ? $(this).parent().find('.height_ft').val() : 0;
		var inch = $(this).parent().find('.height_in').val() > 0 ? parseInt($(this).parent().find('.height_in').val()) : 0;
			
		if (ft > 0 || inch > 0) {		
			$(this).parent().find('.height').val(Math.round((ft * 12 + inch) * 2.54));		
		}	
	});
	$('.height').on('input', function() {
		var height = $(this).val();
		
		if (height > 0) {		
			var ft = parseInt(height / 30.48);
			var inch = Math.round((height / 30.48 - parseInt(height / 30.48)) * 12);
			$(this).parent().find('.height_ft').val(ft);		
			$(this).parent().find('.height_in').val(inch);		
		}	
	});
});
</script>
</body>
